Feedback must be from FEEDBACK_METHODS\n            for ex in week_info['exercises']:\n                self.assertIn(ex['feedback'], FEEDBACK_METHODS)\n            # Support must be from FOLLOW_UP_SUPPORT\n            for support in week_info['follow_up_support']:\n                self.assertIn(support, FOLLOW_UP_SUPPORT)\n\n    def test_generate_roadmap_invalid_date(self):\n        # Description matches\n            self.assertEqual(week[\"description\"], LESSON_TOPICS[i][\"description\"])\n            # Live session matches\n            self.assertEqual(week[\"live_session\"], LESSON_TOPICS[i][\"live_session\"])\n            # Exercises personalized\n            self.assertEqual(len(week[\"exercises\"]), len(LESSON_TOPICS[i][\"exercises\"]))\n            for ex in week[\"exercises\"]:\n                self.assertIn(ex[\"exercise\"], LESSON_TOPICS[i][\"exercises\"])\n                self.assertIn(ex[\"feedback\"], FEEDBACK_METHODS)\n            # Roadmap feedback/support should change if random seed changes\n        random.seed(1)\n        roadmap1 = generate_roadmap(\"Eve\", \"2024-06-01\")\n        random.seed(2)\n        roadmap2 = generate_roadmap(\"Eve\", \"2024-06-01\")\n        #
